ةيصوصخلا كاهتناو تانايبلا مادختسا ةءاسإ :اكيتيلانأ جديربماك ةحيضف 
ةعانصلا نم ةلاح تاسارد :فيظوتلا تايمزراوخ يف زيحتلا 

يعانطصلاا ءاكذلا جذومن رشنو Kubernetes ةعومجم دادعإ – Kubernetes عم لمعلا 
.Deploymentsو Pods مادختساب

.ةددعتلما تابلطلا ةجلاعلم نزاوتلا ليمحتو

Tools & Platforms for MLOps Practice
a. MLflow – https://mlflow.org
– Open-source platform for managing the ML lifecycle: experiment tracking, model packaging, and deployment.
b. DVC (Data Version Control) – https://dvc.org
– A version control system for machine learning projects. Useful for managing data, models, and experiments.
c. Kubeflow – https://www.kubeflow.org
– A Kubernetes-native platform for ML pipelines and workflows in production environments.
6.
d. Weights & Biases – https://wandb.ai
– A powerful tool for experiment tracking, visualization, and collaboration.
e. Google MLOps: Continuous delivery and automation pipelines in machine learning
– https://cloud.google.com/architecture/mlops-continuous-delivery-and-automation-pipelines-in-machine-learning
– This document discusses techniques for implementing and automating continuous integration (CI), continuous
delivery (CD), and continuous training (CT) for machine learning (ML) systems. This document applies primarily to
predictive AI systems.
